# Umbraco
Migration Umbraco 7 to 8

Problem upgrading from Umbraco 7.15.3 to Umbraco 8 (any version) on SQL Server. 
I did it according to the instructions - https://our.umbraco.com/documentation/getting-started/setup/upgrading/migrating-to-v8.
First I updated it to 7.15.7, then to 8.1.0. Used the Pre-migration health checks plugin to check the health before migration. 
There are no problems with a test new project, the migration works
7.15.3 to Umbraco 8 (any version), both SQL CE and SQL Server. When migrating, the following error takes off:
Swears at the absence of the following fields:
mandatoryMessage
validationRegExpMessage
labelOnTop
